Commands.Sql\ChangeLog.md:* Updated Set-AzureRmSqlServerAuditing and Set-AzureRmSqlDatabaseAuditing Cmdlets
Commands.Sql\ChangeLog.md:	- Adding Get-AzureRmSqlServerAuditing cmdlet which gets the auditing settings of an Azure SQL server.
Commands.Sql\ChangeLog.md:	- Adding Set-AzureRmSqlServerAuditing cmdlet which changes the auditing settings of an Azure SQL server.
Commands.Sql\ChangeLog.md:	- Deprecating Get-AzureRmSqlServerAuditingPolicy
Commands.Sql\ChangeLog.md:	- Deprecating Set-AzureRmSqlServerAuditingPolicy
Commands.Sql\ChangeLog.md:	- Deprecating Use-AzureRmSqlServerAuditingPolicy
Commands.Sql\ChangeLog.md:	- Deprecating Remove-AzureRmSqlServerAuditing
Commands.Sql\ChangeLog.md:* Added new return parameter "AuditType" to Get-AzureRmSqlDatabaseAuditingPolicy and Get-AzureRmSqlServerAuditingPolicy returned object
